                Event.observe(window,'click',function(event){  
                        /* Changed by BC : NG : on 4-3-2015 : To resolved issue of google translate block hide in chrome */
                        
                        /*if (event.target.id!='openTranslate' ){
                            $('googleTranslate').style.display = 'none';
                        } */

                            $('googleTranslate').style.display = 'none';
                        }
                        
                        /* End : To resolved issue of google translate block hide in chrome */

    Varien.Tabs = Class.create();
    Varien.Tabs.prototype = {
        initialize: function(selector) {
            var self=this;
            $$(selector+' a').each(this.initTab.bind(this));
        },

        initTab: function(el) {
            //el.href = 'javascript:void(0)';
            if ($(el.parentNode).hasClassName('active')) {
                this.showContent(el);
            }
            el.observe('mouseover', this.showContent.bind(this, el));
        },

        showContent: function(a) {
            var li = $(a.parentNode), ul = $(li.parentNode);
            ul.select('li').each(function(el){
                    var contents = $(el.id+'_contents');
                    if (el==li) {
                        el.addClassName('active');
                        contents.show();
                    } else {
                        el.removeClassName('active');
                        contents.hide();
                    }
            });
        }
    }
    new Varien.Tabs('.product-tabs');
    //]]&gt;
    </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function catalogurlredirect(url)
    {
        window.location = url;
    }

    function checkaddtocart(product_id,type_flg){
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
        $('acp-overlay').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
        $('acp-overlay').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').setStyle({height: 'auto',width: 'auto', left: '651.5px', top: '309.5px'});
        var flag = true;
        var product_array = [];
        var item = {};
        //var product_id = '';
        var temp_product_id = '';
        var temp_product_url = '';
        $$('.ajax-qty').each(function(index,val){
                var item_qty = $(index).value;
                if (item_qty!=''){
                    flag = false;
                    temp_product_id = $(index).id.split("_")[2];
                    //temp_product_url = $('hd_super_group_'+temp_product_id).value;
                    item = {
                        product_id : temp_product_id,
                        qty : item_qty
                        //url : temp_product_url+"qty/"+item_qty
                    };
                    product_array.push(item);
                }
        });

        if (product_id){
            if (type_flg==1)
                item_qty = $('qty_'+product_id).value;
            else if (type_flg==2)
                item_qty = $('qty'+product_id).value;
            else
                item_qty = $('qty').value;
            item = {
                product_id : product_id,
                qty : item_qty
                //url : temp_product_url+"qty/"+item_qty
            };
            flag = false;
            product_array.push(item);
        }

        if (flag){
            alert("Please enter quantity first.");
            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
            $('acp-overlay').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
            return false;
        }else{
            /*for (var i=0;i &lt; product_array.length;i++){
            setLocation(product_array[i]['url']);
            }*/
            var url = 'http://www.sciencix.com/ajaxcartpro/ajax/addmultiple/';
            var params = {};
            params['products'] = Object.toJSON(product_array);
            /*var parameters = {
            products : params
            }*/
            new Ajax.Request(url, {
                    method: 'post',
                    onSuccess: function(transport) {
                        //debugger;
                        if(transport.status == 200) {
                            var response                            =   transport.responseText;
                            response                                =   response.evalJSON();
                            if (response.error){
                                alert(response.error);
                            }else{
                                $$('.header ul.links li.hilight-lnk')[0].innerHTML = response.topLinks;
                                evalScripts(response.topLinks);
                            }
                            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').setStyle({height: 'auto',width: 'auto', left: '651.5px', top: '309.5px'});
                            $('acp-overlay').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');                            

                            /*$('div_document_note').innerHTML        =   response['UCMODOCNOTES'];
                            $('div_m1_description').innerHTML       =   response['cmoLongDescriptionText'];*/
                        }
                    },
                    parameters:params
            }); 
        }
    }
    function evalScripts(html){
        var scripts = html.extractScripts();
        scripts.each(function(script){
                try {
                    //FIX CDATA comment
                    script = script.replace('//&lt;![CDATA[', '').replace('//]]&gt;', '');
                    script = script.replace('/*&lt;![CDATA[*/', '').replace('/*]]&gt;*/', '');
                    eval(script.replace(/var /gi, ""));
                }
                catch(e){
                    if(window.console) {
                        console.log(e.message);
                    }
                }
        });
    }
    function removeproductfromcart(item_id){
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
        $('acp-overlay').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
        $('acp-overlay').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
        $('ajaxcartpro-progress').setStyle({height: 'auto',width: 'auto', left: '651.5px', top: '309.5px'});
        var url = 'http://www.sciencix.com/ajaxcartpro/ajax/removeproductfromcart/';
        var parameters = {
            item_id : item_id
        }
        new Ajax.Request(url, {
                method: 'post',
                onSuccess: function(transport) {
                    //debugger;
                    if(transport.status == 200) {
                        var response                            =   transport.responseText;
                        response                                =   response.evalJSON();
                        if (response.error){
                            alert(response.error);
                        }else{
                            $$('.header ul.links li.hilight-lnk')[0].innerHTML = response.topLinks;
                            evalScripts(response.topLinks);
                            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-progress').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-hide');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').addClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
                            $('ajaxcartpro-add-confirm').setStyle({height: 'auto',width: 'auto', left: '651.5px', top: '309.5px'});
                            $('acp-overlay').removeClassName('ajaxcartpro-box-show');
                        }
                    }
                },
                parameters:parameters
        }); 
    }
    </script>

           function showPdf(iframeName){
        if($(iframeName)==null) {
            alert("PDF not available.");
        } else {
            $(iframeName).style.display="block";
        }
    }

    function hidePdf(iframeName){
        if($(iframeName)==null) {
            alert("PDF not available.");
        } else {
            $(iframeName).style.display="none";
        }

       document.observe("dom:loaded", function() {
                                    var sidebar =  $$("div.col-left");
                                    var allblock=sidebar[0].childElements();
                                    var i = 0;
                                    allblock.each(function(e){
                                            //alert(e.hasClassName('block'))
                                            if(e.hasClassName('block')){
                                                if(i%2 == 0)
                                                    {
                                                    e.addClassName('odd');
                                                }
                                                else
                                                    {
                                                    e.addClassName('even');
                                                }
                                                i++;

                                            }

                                    });
                            });

  (function() {
    function loadChartbeat() {
      window._sf_endpt = (new Date()).getTime();
      var e = document.createElement('script');
      e.setAttribute('language', 'javascript');
      e.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
      e.setAttribute('src','//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat.js');
      document.body.appendChild(e);
    };
    var oldonload = window.onload;
    window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function') ?
      loadChartbeat : function() { oldonload(); loadChartbeat(); };
  })();
  </script>
  <script>
   function decorateList(list, nonRecursive) {
                if ($(list)) {
                    if (typeof(nonRecursive) == 'undefined') {
                        var items = $(list).select('li')
                    }
                    else {
                        var items = $(list).childElements();
                    }
                    decorateGeneric(items, ['odd', 'even', 'last']);
                }
            }
  </script>
